        :prompt "What is your age? [Open-ended]" .

## Q-Gender ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
:QGender  rdf:type :Question ;
          :prompt "What is your gender? [MCQ]" ;
          :hasOption :Gender_A , :Gender_B .

:Gender_A rdf:type :Option ; :code "A" ; :text "Female" .
:Gender_B rdf:type :Option ; :code "B" ; :text "Male"   .

## Q-Blood Type ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
:QBloodType  rdf:type :Question ;
             :prompt "What is your blood type? [MCQ]" ;
             :hasOption :BT_A , :BT_B , :BT_C , :BT_D , :BT_E , :BT_F , :BT_G , :BT_H .

:BT_A  rdf:type :Option ; :code "A" ; :text "A+"  .
:BT_B  rdf:type :Option ; :code "B" ; :text "A-"  .
:BT_C  rdf:type :Option ; :code "C" ; :text "AB+" .
:BT_D  rdf:type :Option ; :code "D" ; :text "AB-" .
:BT_E  rdf:type :Option ; :code "E" ; :text "B+"  .
:BT_F  rdf:type :Option ; :code "F" ; :text "B-"  .
:BT_G  rdf:type :Option ; :code "G" ; :text "O+"  .
:BT_H  rdf:type :Option ; :code "H" ; :text "O-"  .
